V červnu 1968 vydání Scientific American, Martin Gardner popsal ve své \"Matematické Games\" sloupec hru Cl Bakera, který je podobný FreeCell, kromě toho, že karty na tablo jsou postaveny barvy spíše než alternativními barvami. Gardner napsal: \"Hra byla učil Baker jeho otec, který na oplátku ji naučil od Angličana v roce 1920.\" Tato varianta se nyní nazývá Baker je hra. Freecell původy mohou se datují ještě do roku 1945, a skandinávský hra s názvem Napoleon v St. Helena (nikoliv hra Napoleon u St. Helena, také známý jako čtyřicet loupežníků).\r\n\r\nPaul Alfille změnil Bakerův hru tím, že karty stavět podle alternativních barvách, tak vytvářet FreeCell. On realizovala první počítačovou verzi tom v TUTOR programovacího jazyka pro PLATO vzdělávacího počítačového systému v roce 1978. Alfille byl schopen snadno zobrazit rozpoznatelné grafické obrázky hrací karty na displeji 512 * 512 monochromatické na PLATO systémech.\r\n\r\nTento originální FreeCell prostředí povolena hry s 4C10 sloupy a 1C10 buněk kromě standardního 8 * 4 hru. Pro každou variantu, program uložený seřazených seznam hráčů, s nejdelší vítězné pruhy. Tam byl také turnaj systém, který dovolil lidem soutěžit vyhrát obtížné ručně vybral nabídky. Pavel Alfille popisuje tuto časnou FreeCell prostředí podrobněji v rozhovoru z roku 2000.\r\n\r\n\r\nŘešitel složitost\r\nFreeCell Hra má konstantní počet karet. To znamená, že v konstantním čase, člověk nebo počítačový mohli vyjmenovat všech možných tahů z dané konfiguraci začátku a objevte vítěznou sadu pohybů, nebo za předpokladu, že hru nelze řešit, je jeho nedostatek. Chcete-li provést zajímavou složitost analýzu je třeba postavit všeobecný verzi hry FreeCell se 4 * n karet. Tato zobecněná verze hry je NP-úplný; to je nepravděpodobné, že by jakýkoli algoritmus efektivnější než hledání brute-force existuje, které můžete najít řešení pro svévolné všeobecných konfigurace FreeCell.\r\n\r\nExistují 52! is one of the most played board games in the world, play with your friends, try to defeat your opponents with strategy, reasoning and a little bit of luck.\r\nGeneral rules of dominoes:\r\n- Blocking game\r\nThe most basic dominos variant is for two players and requires a double six set. The 28 domino tiles are shuffled face down and form the stock or boneyard. Each player draws seven tiles; the remainder are not used. Once the players begin drawing tiles, they are typically placed on-edge before the players, so that each player can see his own domino tiles, but none can see the value of other players' tiles. Every player can thus see how many tiles remain in the other players' hands at all times during gameplay. One player begins by downing (playing the first tile) one of their tiles. In different games first tiles are also different. In Muggins player should start with the highest double (6-6), in Bergen the first move should be 0-0, in Mexican train each round starts with the next lower double. This tile starts the line of play, a series of tiles in which adjacent tiles touch with matching, i.e. equal, values. The players alternately extend the line of play with one tile at one of its two ends. The game ends when one player wins by playing their last tile, or when the game is blocked because neither player can play. If that occurs, whoever caused the block gets all of the remaining player points not counting their own.\r\n- Scoring game\r\nPlayers accrue points during game play for certain configurations, moves, or emptying one's hand. Most scoring games use variations of the draw game. In Muggins (All fives) player must make the open ends of the layout add up to 5s or a multiple of five (5s, 10, 15, 20, etc.) In bergen player scores when numbers on the open ends are equal. If a player does not call \"domino\" before the tile is laid on the table, and another player says 'domino' after the tile is laid, the first player must pick up an extra domino. In Mexican train the double zero domino is scored as 50 points.\r\n- Draw game\r\nIn a draw game (blocking or scoring), players are additionally allowed to draw as many tiles as desired from the stock before playing a tile. The score of a game is the number of pips in the losing player's hand plus the number of pips in the stock. Most rules prescribe that two tiles need to remain in the stock. The Draw game is often referred to as simply \"dominos\".\r\n\r\nIf you like board games like Checkers, Mahjong, Backgammon and Chess, you will love Dominoes: Best Classic Dominoes Board Game.","ProductFamilyName":"Games","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9MTDJMPVNKN2","TileLayout":"Poster","Title":"Basketball Shoot NBA Stars","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.3647.13809967470494297.62c20468-ccea-4166-9351-1ba5cbda6181.6ea37e8b-4fe8-43f3-adbf-8209479a6f85","Height":300,"Width":300,"BackgroundColor":"#ffffff","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.47031.13809967470494297.62c20468-ccea-4166-9351-1ba5cbda6181.6a70d50a-0a62-4f4f-865b-fb78bb74c1fd","Height":300,"Width":620,"BackgroundColor":"#ffffff","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"Zdarma","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":0.0,"RatingsCount":"0","PackageFamilyNames":["23790BitMangoGames.BasketballShootNBAStars_zcfjb2tswwhgj"],"ContentIds":["f7c07237-0bab-a9e6-968a-63f480e5da47","ac5b7951-e4b5-a21c-8d56-4e407a6d7445"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"Počítač","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Like scoring the baskets in basketball?
